		<div id="mw-indicator-noteTA-2b411986" class="mw-indicator"><div class="mw-parser-output"><span typeof="mw:File"><span title="本页使用了标题或全文手工转换"><img alt="本页使用了标题或全文手工转换" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Zh_conversion_icon_m.svg/35px-Zh_conversion_icon_m.svg.png" decoding="async" width="35" height="22" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Zh_conversion_icon_m.svg/53px-Zh_conversion_icon_m.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Zh_conversion_icon_m.svg/70px-Zh_conversion_icon_m.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="32" data-file-height="20" /></span></span></div></div>

					<div id="contentSub" lang="zh-Hans-CN" dir="ltr"><div id="mw-content-subtitle" lang="zh-Hans-CN" dir="ltr"><span class="mw-redirectedfrom">（重定向自<a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%94%B5%E5%AE%B9&amp;redirect=no" class="mw-redirect" title="电容">电容</a>）</span></div></div>
					
					
					<div id="mw-content-text" class="mw-body-content"><div class="mw-content-ltr mw-parser-output" lang="zh-Hans-CN" dir="ltr"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E6%B6%88%E6%AD%A7%E4%B9%89" title="Wikipedia:消歧义"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Disambig_gray.svg/25px-Disambig_gray.svg.png" decoding="async" width="25" height="19" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Disambig_gray.svg/38px-Disambig_gray.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Disambig_gray.svg/50px-Disambig_gray.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="220" data-file-height="168" /></a></span><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r74069148">body:not(.skin-minerva) .mw-parser-output .ifmobile>.mobile{display:none}body.skin-minerva .mw-parser-output .ifmobile>.nomobile{display:inherit;display:initial}</style><span class="ifmobile"><span class="nomobile">&#160;&#160;</span><span class="mobile"></span></span>此条目页的主题是物理量。关于电路元件，请见“<b><a href="/wiki/%E7%94%B5%E5%AE%B9%E5%99%A8" title="电容器">电容器</a></b>”。</div>
<table class="box-Cleanup-jargon plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-style" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Edit-clear.svg/40px-Edit-clear.svg.png" decoding="async" width="40" height="40" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Edit-clear.svg/60px-Edit-clear.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Edit-clear.svg/80px-Edit-clear.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="48" data-file-height="48" /></span></span></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><span class="mbox-text-span">此条目<b>包含过多<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E8%A1%8C%E8%AF%9D%E8%A7%A3%E9%87%8A" title="Wikipedia:行话解释">行话或专业术语</a>，可能需要简化或提出进一步解释。</b><span class="hide-when-compact"></span> <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">2017年4月20日</span>)</i></small><span class="hide-when-compact"><br /><small>请在<a href="/wiki/Talk:%E9%9B%BB%E5%AE%B9" title="Talk:电容">讨论页</a>中发表对于本议题的看法，并移除或解释本条目中的行话。</small></span><span class="hide-when-compact"></span></span></td></tr></tbody></table>
<div id="noteTA-2b411986" class="noteTA"><div class="noteTA-group"><div data-noteta-group-source="module" data-noteta-group="Physics"></div></div><div class="noteTA-local"><div data-noteta-code="纳法拉=&gt;zh-tw:奈法拉;纳法拉=&gt;zh-hant:奈法拉"></div></div></div>
<figure class="mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Capacitor.png" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b5/Capacitor.png/200px-Capacitor.png" decoding="async" width="200" height="250" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b5/Capacitor.png 1.5x" data-file-width="275" data-file-height="344" /></a><figcaption>感受到<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E5%AE%B9%E5%99%A8" class="mw-redirect" title="电容器">电容器</a>两端的<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E4%BD%8D%E5%B7%AE" class="mw-redirect" title="电势差">电势差</a>，正电荷与负电荷会分别累积于两片平行薄板导体。</figcaption></figure>
<p>在<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E8%B7%AF%E5%AD%B8" class="mw-redirect" title="电路学">电路学</a>里，给定<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E5%A3%93" title="电压">电压</a>，<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E5%AE%B9%E5%99%A8" class="mw-redirect" title="电容器">电容器</a>储存<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E8%8D%B7" title="电荷">电荷</a>的能力，称为<b>电容</b>（英语：<span lang="en">capacitance</span>），标记为<b>C</b>。采用<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%8B%E9%9A%9B%E5%96%AE%E4%BD%8D%E5%88%B6" class="mw-redirect" title="国际单位制">国际单位制</a>，电容的单位是<a href="/wiki/%E6%B3%95%E6%8B%89" title="法拉">法拉</a>（<span lang="en">farad</span>），标记为<b>F</b>。
</p><p>平行板<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E5%AE%B9%E5%99%A8" class="mw-redirect" title="电容器">电容器</a>是一种简单的电容器，是由互相平行、以空间或<a href="/wiki/%E4%BB%8B%E9%9B%BB%E8%B3%AA" title="介电质">介电质</a>隔离的两片薄板<a href="/wiki/%E5%B0%8E%E9%AB%94" class="mw-redirect" title="导体">导体</a>构成。假设这两片导板分别载有负电荷与正电荷，所载有的电荷量分别为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle -Q\,\!}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
        <mi>Q</mi>
        <mspace width="thinmathspace" />
        <mspace width="negativethinmathspace" />
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle -Q\,\!}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/13fd0f0f4bbf05b4f4c2f51af48c002ef997214c" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-right: -0.387ex; width:4.034ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle -Q\,\!}"></span>、<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle +Q\,\!}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mo>+</mo>
        <mi>Q</mi>
        <mspace width="thinmathspace" />
        <mspace width="negativethinmathspace" />
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle +Q\,\!}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6b06a102be78feacde7ae33c474a2c104933100f" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-right: -0.387ex; width:4.034ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle +Q\,\!}"></span>，两片导板之间的电势差为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle V}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>V</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle V}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/af0f6064540e84211d0ffe4dac72098adfa52845" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.787ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle V}"></span>，则这电容器的电容<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle C}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>C</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle C}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4fc55753007cd3c18576f7933f6f089196732029" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.766ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle C}"></span>为
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle C={\frac {Q}{V}}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>C</mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mfrac>
            <mi>Q</mi>
            <mi>V</mi>
          </mfrac>
        </mrow>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle C={\frac {Q}{V}}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/69c105c2c94d7e78f0556c93c3632186ec717d89" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:7.539ex; height:5.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle C={\frac {Q}{V}}}"></span>。</dd></dl>
<p>由上式知1法拉（Farad）等于1<a href="/wiki/%E5%BA%AB%E4%BE%96" class="mw-redirect" title="库仑">库仑</a>（Coulomb）每<a href="/wiki/%E4%BC%8F%E7%89%B9" title="伏特">伏特</a>（Voltage）。在正常状况下1法拉的电容多加1伏特的电势差可以多储存1库仑的电荷。
</p><p>电容器所储存的能量等于充电所做的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8A%9F" title="功">功</a>。思考前述平行板电容器，搬移微小电荷元素<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} q}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
        </mrow>
        <mi>q</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} q}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/35c5e5a60fd86bfd1354b8f22ef6dbbdbbf014a4" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.362ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} q}"></span>从带负电薄板到带正电薄板，每对抗1伏特的电势差，需要做功<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} W}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
        </mrow>
        <mi>W</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} W}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/13013d9267b5797a073fa53a404f27af9cd756d6" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:3.728ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} W}"></span>：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} W={\frac {q}{C}}\,\mathrm {d} q}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
        </mrow>
        <mi>W</mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mfrac>
            <mi>q</mi>
            <mi>C</mi>
          </mfrac>
        </mrow>
        <mspace width="thinmathspace" />
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
        </mrow>
        <mi>q</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} W={\frac {q}{C}}\,\mathrm {d} q}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cb3875b41e722a2f653af4bed59c4b4e43cb420f" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:12.178ex; height:5.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} W={\frac {q}{C}}\,\mathrm {d} q}"></span>。</dd></dl>
<p>将这方程积分，可以得到储存于电容器的能量。从尚未充电的电容器（<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle q=0}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>q</mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle q=0}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/654c2d5dc1a26e0af36dc0deb5fd252c6178977a" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:5.33ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle q=0}"></span>）开始，搬移电荷从带负电薄板到带正电薄板，直到这两片薄板分别拥有电荷量<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle -Q}">
  <semantics>

      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle -Q}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3ff459062914e488a99e0f453ee6fe6b1315a34d" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:3.646ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle -Q}"></span>、<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle +Q}">

<meta property="mw:PageProp/toc" />
<h2><span id=".E5.8D.95.E4.BD.8D"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="单位">单位</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%BB%E5%AE%B9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="编辑章节：单位"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E6%B3%95%E6%8B%89" title="法拉">法拉</a></div>
<p>电容的单位是法拉，简称“法”，单位符号为“F”，是<a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%BD%E9%99%85%E5%8D%95%E4%BD%8D%E5%88%B6%E5%AF%BC%E5%87%BA%E5%8D%95%E4%BD%8D" title="国际单位制导出单位">国际单位制导出单位</a><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>。与其他物理量的关系：一法拉等于一<a href="/wiki/%E5%BA%AB%E4%BE%96" class="mw-redirect" title="库仑">库仑</a>除以一<a href="/wiki/%E4%BC%8F%E7%89%B9" title="伏特">伏特</a>。一般来说，1法拉算是很大的电容，大多数用于<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E5%AD%90%E9%9B%BB%E8%B7%AF" title="电子电路">电子电路</a>的电容器，其电容会小于法拉几个数量级，常用的单位有“微法拉”（microfarad，μF），等于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle 10^{-6}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <msup>
          <mn>10</mn>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
            <mn>6</mn>
          </mrow>
        </msup>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 10^{-6}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/70b5788b8e24bbc50c5c6fc7b5ef4953cb2291e0" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:4.658ex; height:2.676ex;" alt="{\displaystyle 10^{-6}}"></span>法拉；以及“纳法拉”（nanofarad，nF），等于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle 10^{-9}}">
  <semantics>

          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
            <mn>9</mn>
          </mrow>
        </msup>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 10^{-9}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/69ad2ba4cbe9e68b60b98de6b2875625abb3b446" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:4.658ex; height:2.676ex;" alt="{\displaystyle 10^{-9}}"></span>法拉。在<a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E6%B3%A2" title="微波">微波</a>工程领域中，有时会使用到较小的“皮法拉”（picofarad，pF），等于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle 10^{-12}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <msup>
          <mn>10</mn>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
            <mn>12</mn>
          </mrow>
        </msup>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 10^{-12}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bba598fb9ea212852e9cfe571d5dbbf1892c285d" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.48ex; height:2.676ex;" alt="{\displaystyle 10^{-12}}"></span>法拉；甚至更小的“飞法拉”（femtofarad，fF），等于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle 10^{-15}}">

<h2><span id=".E9.9B.BB.E5.AE.B9.E5.99.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="電容器">电容器</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%BB%E5%AE%B9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="编辑章节：电容器"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E5%AE%B9%E5%99%A8" class="mw-redirect" title="电容器">电容器</a></div>
<p>假设，给定电容器的几何形状和电容器内部的介质性质，则可以计算出电容。如前图所示，假设平行板电容器的两片导板的面积都是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle A}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>A</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle A}"></span>，间隔距离为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle d}">

  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \sigma =Q/A}">

<p>应用<a href="/wiki/%E9%AB%98%E6%96%AF%E5%AE%9A%E5%BE%8B" title="高斯定律">高斯定律</a>（详尽细节，请参阅条目<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E4%BD%8D%E7%A7%BB#應用範例" title="电位移">电位移</a>），在两片导板之间的<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E5%A0%B4" title="电场">电场</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle E}">

<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle E=\sigma /\varepsilon =Q/\varepsilon A}">

        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle E=\sigma /\varepsilon =Q/\varepsilon A}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f940686b893b0e9c5633a9052741bb65ff71fc5b" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:17.376ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle E=\sigma /\varepsilon =Q/\varepsilon A}"></span>；</dd></dl>
<p>其中，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \varepsilon }">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>&#x03B5;<!-- ε --></mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \varepsilon }</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a30c89172e5b88edbd45d3e2772c7f5e562e5173" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.083ex; height:1.676ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \varepsilon }"></span>是介质的<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%B5%E5%AE%B9%E7%8E%87" title="电容率">电容率</a>。
</p><p>两片导板的电势差为
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle V=Ed=\sigma d/\varepsilon =Qd/\varepsilon A}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>V</mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mi>E</mi>
        <mi>d</mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mi>&#x03C3;<!-- σ --></mi>
        <mi>d</mi>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo>/</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mi>&#x03B5;<!-- ε --></mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mi>Q</mi>
        <mi>d</mi>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo>/</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mi>&#x03B5;<!-- ε --></mi>
        <mi>A</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle V=Ed=\sigma d/\varepsilon =Qd/\varepsilon A}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/857f89b4ae5be0e81e8719c1eb1506bbbeeac65a" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:25.909ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle V=Ed=\sigma d/\varepsilon =Qd/\varepsilon A}"></span>。</dd></dl>
<p>所以，电容为
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle C=Q/V=\varepsilon A/d}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>C</mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mi>Q</mi>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo>/</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mi>V</mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mi>&#x03B5;<!-- ε --></mi>
        <mi>A</mi>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo>/</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mi>d</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle C=Q/V=\varepsilon A/d}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/186ef515cd034ce4dbe0f16a59f399c2a4e9211a" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:17.956ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle C=Q/V=\varepsilon A/d}"></span>。</dd></dl>
<p>电容与导板面积A成正比，与导板间隔距离d呈反比，这是在假设平板电容器的面积A相当大的情况下，可以忽略电容器边缘的效应。假设间隔距离<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle d}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>d</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle d}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e85ff03cbe0c7341af6b982e47e9f90d235c66ab" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.216ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle d}"></span>远小于导板的长度与宽度，则上述方程乃优良近似；在电容器内大部分区域的电场是均匀的；在电容器周围的边缘电场只给出很小贡献，可以被忽略。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E9.9B.BB.E5.A3.93.E4.BE.9D.E8.B3.B4.E6.80.A7.E9.9B.BB.E5.AE.B9.E5.99.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="電壓依賴性電容器">电压依赖性电容器</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%BB%E5%AE%B9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="编辑章节：电压依赖性电容器"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Ferroelectric_polarisation.svg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Ferroelectric_polarisation.svg/200px-Ferroelectric_polarisation.svg.png" decoding="async" width="200" height="201" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Ferroelectric_polarisation.svg/300px-Ferroelectric_polarisation.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Ferroelectric_polarisation.svg/400px-Ferroelectric_polarisation.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="160" data-file-height="161" /></a><figcaption>铁电性物质的<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E6%A5%B5%E5%8C%96%E5%BC%B7%E5%BA%A6" class="mw-redirect" title="电极化强度">电极化强度</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle P}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>P</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle P}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b4dc73bf40314945ff376bd363916a738548d40a" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.745ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle P}"></span>对电场<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle E}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>E</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle E}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4232c9de2ee3eec0a9c0a19b15ab92daa6223f9b" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.776ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle E}"></span>的曲线显示出<a href="/wiki/%E9%81%B2%E6%BB%AF%E7%8F%BE%E8%B1%A1" title="迟滞现象">迟滞现象</a>。</figcaption></figure>
<p>许多常用的电介质，其<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%B5%E5%AE%B9%E7%8E%87" title="电容率">电容率</a>会随着外电场的变化而改变，是外电场的函数。<a href="/wiki/%E9%93%81%E7%94%B5%E6%80%A7" title="铁电性">铁电性</a>物质就是这种电介质。使用这种电介质的电容器，其电容会比较复杂。例如，当这种电容器在充电时，电荷与电压（电势差）的关系为
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} Q=C(V)\ \mathrm {d} V}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
        </mrow>
        <mi>Q</mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mi>C</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>V</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mtext>&#xA0;</mtext>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
        </mrow>
        <mi>V</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} Q=C(V)\ \mathrm {d} V}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d0247a3ecabcab97d096827440cd5b0168a93c85" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:15.253ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} Q=C(V)\ \mathrm {d} V}"></span>。</dd></dl>
<p>在上述方程里，电容对于电压的依赖性<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle C(V)}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>C</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>V</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle C(V)}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/41c4cecddccf29a31848fb521b2408c8958b720f" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.363ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle C(V)}"></span>，是因为电场产生的。一个平行板电容器的电场为
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle E=V/d}">
  <semantics>

      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

        <mo>=</mo>
        <mi>V</mi>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo>/</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mi>d</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle E=V/d}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/41f15e903d7ebd822c0d45550f96434c328ddb5a" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:9.04ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle E=V/d}"></span>。</dd></dl>
<p>这电场将电介质电极化，从而增加导板储存电荷的能力。如右图所示，对于铁电性物质，<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E6%A5%B5%E5%8C%96%E5%BC%B7%E5%BA%A6" class="mw-redirect" title="电极化强度">电极化强度</a>对电场曲线显示出<a href="/wiki/%E9%81%B2%E6%BB%AF%E7%8F%BE%E8%B1%A1" title="迟滞现象">迟滞现象</a><sup id="cite_ref-Araujo_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Araujo-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Musikant_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Musikant-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>。这是一个非线性关系。
</p><p>假设<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E6%A5%B5%E5%8C%96%E5%BC%B7%E5%BA%A6" class="mw-redirect" title="电极化强度">电极化强度</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle P}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>P</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle P}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b4dc73bf40314945ff376bd363916a738548d40a" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.745ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle P}"></span>与电场、电压的关系为
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle P=f(E)=f(V/d)=g(V)}">

<p>其中，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle f(E)}">

</p><p>根据电位移<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle D}">

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle D=P+\epsilon _{0}E=g(V)+\epsilon _{0}V/d}">

<p>应用<a href="/wiki/%E9%AB%98%E6%96%AF%E5%AE%9A%E5%BE%8B" title="高斯定律">自由电荷高斯定律</a>，导板载有的电荷量为
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle Q=DA=(g(V)+\epsilon _{0}V/d)A}">

    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle Q=DA=(g(V)+\epsilon _{0}V/d)A}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/dc4f6e80b5761c2be1100736587b2be3a1d0c71b" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:28.972ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle Q=DA=(g(V)+\epsilon _{0}V/d)A}"></span>。</dd></dl>
<p>所以，电容为
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle C(V)={\frac {Q}{V}}={\frac {g(V)A}{V}}+{\frac {\epsilon _{0}A}{d}}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>C</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>V</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mfrac>
            <mi>Q</mi>
            <mi>V</mi>
          </mfrac>
        </mrow>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mfrac>
            <mrow>
              <mi>g</mi>
              <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
              <mi>V</mi>
              <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
              <mi>A</mi>
            </mrow>
            <mi>V</mi>
          </mfrac>
        </mrow>
        <mo>+</mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mfrac>
            <mrow>
              <msub>
                <mi>&#x03F5;<!-- ϵ --></mi>
                <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                  <mn>0</mn>
                </mrow>
              </msub>
              <mi>A</mi>
            </mrow>
            <mi>d</mi>
          </mfrac>
        </mrow>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle C(V)={\frac {Q}{V}}={\frac {g(V)A}{V}}+{\frac {\epsilon _{0}A}{d}}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/991ca17da65f51ba92496da897dcce08f96af275" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:28.944ex; height:5.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle C(V)={\frac {Q}{V}}={\frac {g(V)A}{V}}+{\frac {\epsilon _{0}A}{d}}}"></span>。</dd></dl>
<p>假设<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle g(V)}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>g</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>V</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle g(V)}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/942bfa208ab40e1288ef663be455474f5c4a2f08" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.713ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle g(V)}"></span>是线性函数，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle g(V)=kV}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>g</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>V</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mi>k</mi>
        <mi>V</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle g(V)=kV}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cba738f60832b97976c606f864940ca7f51218c1" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:10.809ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle g(V)=kV}"></span>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle k}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>k</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle k}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c3c9a2c7b599b37105512c5d570edc034056dd40" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.211ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle k}"></span>是常数，则电容与电压无关：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle C={\frac {Q}{V}}=kA+{\frac {\epsilon _{0}A}{d}}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

        <mo>=</mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mfrac>
            <mi>Q</mi>
            <mi>V</mi>
          </mfrac>
        </mrow>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mi>k</mi>
        <mi>A</mi>
        <mo>+</mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mfrac>
            <mrow>

    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle C={\frac {Q}{V}}=kA+{\frac {\epsilon _{0}A}{d}}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e68c6a92c1901f8ae1dd2a5a3c854502af3f8fe7" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:21.01ex; height:5.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle C={\frac {Q}{V}}=kA+{\frac {\epsilon _{0}A}{d}}}"></span>。</dd></dl>
<p>否则，假设<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle g(V)}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>g</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>V</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle g(V)}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/942bfa208ab40e1288ef663be455474f5c4a2f08" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.713ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle g(V)}"></span>是非线性函数，则电容与电压成非线性关系。
</p><p>继续思考这跟电压有关的电容，假若将电容器充电至电压<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle V}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>V</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle V}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/af0f6064540e84211d0ffe4dac72098adfa52845" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.787ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle V}"></span>，则电容器的两片导板会分别带有电量<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle +Q}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mo>+</mo>
        <mi>Q</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle +Q}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/50207f58f170206fc2b7f7117b09c91b36d9cd26" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:3.646ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle +Q}"></span>、<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle -Q}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
        <mi>Q</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle -Q}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3ff459062914e488a99e0f453ee6fe6b1315a34d" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:3.646ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle -Q}"></span>：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle Q=\int _{0}^{V}C(V')\ \mathrm {d} V'}">
  <semantics>

          </mrow>

        </msup>

          <mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
        </mrow>
        <msup>
          <mi>V</mi>
          <mo>&#x2032;</mo>
        </msup>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle Q=\int _{0}^{V}C(V')\ \mathrm {d} V'}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f617324589ad38c115347b40cd8080c538a0539e" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:19.936ex; height:6.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle Q=\int _{0}^{V}C(V&#039;)\ \mathrm {d} V&#039;}"></span>。</dd></dl>
<p>当电容与电压无关时，这方程变为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle Q=CV}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>Q</mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mi>C</mi>
        <mi>V</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle Q=CV}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/21834f0f2e9afa6df07e9517744aa7763b601a02" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:8.49ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle Q=CV}"></span>。
</p><p>储存于<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E5%AE%B9%E5%99%A8" class="mw-redirect" title="电容器">电容器</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E5%88%86" title="微分">微分</a><a href="/wiki/%E8%83%BD%E9%87%8F" title="能量">能量</a>为
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} U_{\text{stored}}=Q\mathrm {d} V''=\left[\int _{0}^{V''}\ C(V')\ \mathrm {d} V'\right]\mathrm {d} V''}">

  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/1eb1d2a38f0054ef11a42860b809646552c2ebac" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -3.171ex; width:43.907ex; height:7.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} U_{\text{stored}}=Q\mathrm {d} V&#039;&#039;=\left[\int _{0}^{V&#039;&#039;}\ C(V&#039;)\ \mathrm {d} V&#039;\right]\mathrm {d} V&#039;&#039;}"></span>。</dd></dl>
<p>应用<a href="/wiki/%E5%88%86%E9%83%A8%E7%A9%8D%E5%88%86%E6%B3%95" title="分部积分法">分部积分法</a>：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \int _{a}^{z}f(x)g'(x)\ \mathrm {d} x=\left[f(x)g(x)\right]_{a}^{z}-\int _{a}^{z}f'(x)g(x)\ \mathrm {d} x}">

  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/69a9b2585fbf8bcdf0ee5d636114b1d4396dcab4" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:49.877ex; height:5.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \int _{a}^{z}f(x)g&#039;(x)\ \mathrm {d} x=\left[f(x)g(x)\right]_{a}^{z}-\int _{a}^{z}f&#039;(x)g(x)\ \mathrm {d} x}"></span>，</dd></dl>
<p>分别设定<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle f(x)=\int _{a}^{x}\ h(y)\ \mathrm {d} y}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>

          <mo>&#x222B;<!-- ∫ --></mo>

          </mrow>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>x</mi>
          </mrow>
        </msubsup>
        <mtext>&#xA0;</mtext>
        <mi>h</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>y</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mtext>&#xA0;</mtext>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
        </mrow>
        <mi>y</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(x)=\int _{a}^{x}\ h(y)\ \mathrm {d} y}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b5e8f7910c6dd90d91ea03f6c18e39fbec97ddc8" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:19.453ex; height:5.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle f(x)=\int _{a}^{x}\ h(y)\ \mathrm {d} y}"></span>、<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle g(x)=x}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>g</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle g(x)=x}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cbbcdeb274573ed78ada04c0038bf0bcb0c6d806" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:8.683ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle g(x)=x}"></span>，带入上述方程，则可得到
</p>

<p><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%8E%83%E6%8F%8F%E9%9D%9E%E7%B7%9A%E6%80%A7%E4%BB%8B%E8%B3%AA%E9%A1%AF%E5%BE%AE%E9%8F%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="扫描非线性介质显微镜（页面不存在）">扫描非线性介质显微镜</a>（<span lang="en">scanning nonlinear dielectric microscope</span>）的探针扫描于铁电性物质表面所测量到的非线性电容，可以用来研究铁电性物质的铁电畴（<span lang="en">ferroelectric domain</span>）结构<sup id="cite_ref-Cho_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cho-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>。
</p><p>有些<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%8A%E5%B0%8E%E9%AB%94%E5%85%83%E4%BB%B6" class="mw-redirect" title="半导体元件">半导体元件</a>的电容可以用电压控制。例如，当<a href="/wiki/%E8%AE%8A%E5%AE%B9%E4%BA%8C%E6%A5%B5%E9%AB%94" title="变容二极管">变容二极管</a>的逆向偏压增加时，空乏层厚度也会增加，因而使得电容降低<sup id="cite_ref-Sze0_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sze0-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E9.A0.BB.E7.8E.87.E4.BE.9D.E8.B3.B4.E6.80.A7.E9.9B.BB.E5.AE.B9.E5.99.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="頻率依賴性電容器">频率依赖性电容器</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%BB%E5%AE%B9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="编辑章节：频率依赖性电容器"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>假若电容器两端驱动的含时电压变化太快，则电介质的电极化强度可能会无法跟上讯号。从微观层次解释这机制，在电介质内部，决定电容率的微小<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E5%81%B6%E6%A5%B5%E5%AD%90" class="mw-redirect" title="电偶极子">电偶极子</a>无法瞬时地移动，因此，当施加的交流电压的频率增加时，电偶极子只能给出有限的响应，从而造成<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%B5%E5%AE%B9%E7%8E%87" title="电容率">电容率</a>降低。电容率与频率的关系称为<a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BB%8B%E9%9B%BB%E8%89%B2%E6%95%A3&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="介电色散（页面不存在）">介电色散</a>（<span lang="en">dielectric dispersion</span>），是由<a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BB%8B%E9%9B%BB%E5%BC%9B%E8%B1%AB&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="介电弛豫（页面不存在）">介电弛豫</a>（<span lang="en">dielectric relaxation</span>）过程所主控，像<a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%B7%E6%8B%9C%E5%BC%9B%E8%B1%AB" class="mw-redirect" title="德拜弛豫">德拜弛豫</a>（<span lang="en">Debye relaxation</span>）。从更基本的微观分析来计算，例如对于介质内的电偶极子行为的微观分析，处于暂态状况，电位移场可以表达为（更详尽细节，请参阅<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E6%A5%B5%E5%8C%96%E7%8E%87" title="电极化率">电极化率</a>）
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle {\boldsymbol {D}}(t)={\frac {\varepsilon _{0}}{\sqrt {2\pi }}}\int _{-\infty }^{t}\mathrm {d} t'\ \varepsilon _{r}(t-t'){\boldsymbol {E}}(t')}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mi mathvariant="bold-italic">D</mi>
        </mrow>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>t</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mfrac>
            <msub>
              <mi>&#x03B5;<!-- ε --></mi>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mn>0</mn>
              </mrow>
            </msub>
            <msqrt>
              <mn>2</mn>
              <mi>&#x03C0;<!-- π --></mi>
            </msqrt>
          </mfrac>
        </mrow>
        <msubsup>
          <mo>&#x222B;<!-- ∫ --></mo>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
            <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x221E;<!-- ∞ --></mi>
          </mrow>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>t</mi>
          </mrow>
        </msubsup>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
        </mrow>
        <msup>
          <mi>t</mi>
          <mo>&#x2032;</mo>
        </msup>
        <mtext>&#xA0;</mtext>
        <msub>
          <mi>&#x03B5;<!-- ε --></mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>r</mi>
          </mrow>
        </msub>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>

</p><p>相对电容率的时间依赖可以用<a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%B7%9A%E6%80%A7%E9%9F%BF%E6%87%89%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="线性响应函数（页面不存在）">线性响应函数</a>（<span lang="en">linear response function</span>）来描述<sup id="cite_ref-Giuliani_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Giuliani-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>。上述方程显示出相对电容率的时间依赖所产生的滞后响应。这积分式的积分域从整个过去历史一直延伸至现时。假设每当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \Delta t&lt;0\,\!}">
  <semantics>

        <mo>&lt;</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mspace width="thinmathspace" />
        <mspace width="negativethinmathspace" />
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>

  </semantics>

</p>

</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/55c9acfeb8e9298b2026f36b1b2d4f5fb3aac494" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.592ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} \mathbf {a} }"></span>是微小面元素。
</p><p>流入闭曲面<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {S} }">

<p>其中，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \varepsilon _{r}'(\omega )}">

        </msub>

    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle C_{0}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/23da38e31194b9ae0524ec18c8489693f3be5389" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.716ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle C_{0}}"></span>是没有电介质时的电容（即平行板电容器的两片导板之间是<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E7%94%B1%E7%A9%BA%E9%96%93" title="自由空间">自由空间</a>时的电容）。
</p><p><a href="/wiki/%E6%B7%B1%E8%83%BD%E7%B4%9A%E6%9A%AB%E6%85%8B%E8%AD%9C%E5%AD%B8" title="深能级暂态谱学">深能级暂态谱学</a>（<span lang="en">deep-level transient spectroscopy</span>）利用电容的时间响应来研究<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%8A%E5%B0%8E%E9%AB%94" class="mw-redirect" title="半导体">半导体</a>的深能级缺陷<sup id="cite_ref-Kasap_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kasap-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>。按照能级在半导体<a href="/wiki/%E8%83%BD%E9%9A%99" title="能隙">能隙</a>的位置，缺陷分类为浅能级缺陷和深能级缺陷。浅能级缺陷的能级离<a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%BC%E5%B8%A6" title="导带">导带</a>或<a href="/wiki/%E5%83%B9%E5%B8%B6" title="价带">价带</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E8%83%BD%E5%B8%A6" class="mw-redirect" title="能带">能带</a>边缘比较近，在0.1eV以内，处于这能级的电子或空穴很容易因热运动而变成自由电子或自由空穴；一般而言，深能级缺陷离能带边缘比较远，超过0.1eV。但也有些物质的深能级缺陷离能带边缘虽然只有0.001eV，仍旧能够显示出深能级缺陷的通常性质<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>。
</p><p><a href="/wiki/%E9%87%91%E5%B1%AC%E6%B0%A7%E5%8C%96%E7%89%A9%E5%8D%8A%E5%B0%8E%E9%AB%94%E9%9B%BB%E5%AE%B9%E5%99%A8" title="金属氧化物半导体电容器">金属氧化物半导体电容器</a>（<span lang="en">MOS capacitor</span>）是另一个电容与频率有关的例子。对于这案例，<a href="/wiki/%E8%BC%89%E6%B5%81%E5%AD%90" class="mw-redirect" title="载流子">少数载流子</a>的缓慢生成意味着在高频率状况，只有<a href="/wiki/%E8%BC%89%E6%B5%81%E5%AD%90" class="mw-redirect" title="载流子">多数载流子</a>的响应能够贡献出电容，而在低频率状况，两种载流子的响应都能够贡献出电容<sup id="cite_ref-Sze_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sze-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Kasap_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kasap-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>。
</p><p>当频率为<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%89%E5%AD%B8" class="mw-redirect" title="光学">光学</a>频率时，<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%8A%E5%B0%8E%E9%AB%94" class="mw-redirect" title="半导体">半导体</a>的电容会展示出类似固体的能带结构。精密的<a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%AA%BF%E5%88%B6%E5%85%89%E8%AD%9C%E5%AD%B8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="调制光谱学（页面不存在）">调制光谱学</a>（<span lang="en">modulation spectroscopy</span>）测量方法，使用<a href="/wiki/%E5%A3%93%E5%8A%9B" class="mw-redirect" title="压力">压力</a>或其它种<a href="/wiki/%E6%87%89%E5%8A%9B" title="应力">应力</a>来调制晶体结构，然后观测光波的吸收或反射的相关变化。这方法贡献出很多关于这些物质的性质的结果<sup id="cite_ref-Cardona_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cardona-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E9.9B.BB.E5.AE.B9.E7.9F.A9.E9.99.A3"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="電容矩陣">电容矩阵</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%BB%E5%AE%B9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：电容矩阵"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>前面论述的范围局限于两片任意尺寸、形状的平行导板的案例。对于单独的带电导板，电容的定义方程<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle C\ {\stackrel {def}{=}}\ Q/V}">

<p>其中，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle P_{ij}}">

    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle P_{ij}}</annotation>

</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/43ef37c239b6d38f1e951a31eb1a3bd295271b40" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:2.969ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle P_{ij}}"></span>是电势系数，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle i,j=1,2,3}">

    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<p>设定第<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle i}">

  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/add78d8608ad86e54951b8c8bd6c8d8416533d20" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.802ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle i}"></span>个导体的电势为1Volt，其它导体的电势为0Volt，则对于这系统，第<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle i}">

  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/add78d8608ad86e54951b8c8bd6c8d8416533d20" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.802ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle i}"></span>个导体的载电量等于其电容。

<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle P_{ij}\ {\stackrel {def}{=}}\ {\frac {\partial V_{i}}{\partial Q_{j}}}}">

  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9857cc48daf6663c4aa8700978db60609b6a8305" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.671ex; width:11.563ex; height:6.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle P_{ij}\ {\stackrel {def}{=}}\ {\frac {\partial V_{i}}{\partial Q_{j}}}}"></span>。</dd></dl>

  <semantics>

          </mfrac>
        </mrow>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle C_{ij}\ {\stackrel {def}{=}}\ {\frac {\partial Q_{i}}{\partial V_{j}}}}</annotation>
  </semantics>

<h2><span id=".E8.87.AA.E9.9B.BB.E5.AE.B9"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="自電容">自电容</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%BB%E5%AE%B9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="编辑章节：自电容"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>在<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E8%B7%AF%E5%AD%B8" class="mw-redirect" title="电路学">电路学</a>里，电容通常是术语“互电容”（<span lang="en">mutual capacitance</span>）的简称，即两个邻近导体（像平行板电容器的两片薄板）之间的电容。另外还有一种电路学性质术语“自电容”（<span lang="en">self-capacitance</span>），即单独导体的电势每增加1V所需的电荷量。设定这电势等于零的参考点为一个理论球壳导体，其半径为无穷远，其球心与单独导体同位置。假设这单独导体是半径为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle R}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>R</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle R}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4b0bfb3769bf24d80e15374dc37b0441e2616e33" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle R}"></span>的球形导体，则其球表面电势为
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle V=Q/4\pi \varepsilon _{0}R}">
  <semantics>

<h3><span id=".E7.AF.84.E4.BE.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="範例">范例</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%BB%E5%AE%B9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：范例"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E8%8C%83%E5%BE%B7%E6%A0%BC%E6%8B%89%E5%A4%AB%E8%B5%B7%E7%94%B5%E6%9C%BA" title="范德格拉夫起电机">范德格拉夫起电机</a>顶端的圆球形金属导体，其半径通常为20&#160;cm，这金属导体的自电容为
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle C=4\pi \varepsilon _{0}R=4\pi \times 8.85\times 10^{-12}\times 0.2\approx 22[pF]}">

<h2><span id=".E9.9B.9C.E6.95.A3.E9.9B.BB.E5.AE.B9"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="雜散電容">杂散电容</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%BB%E5%AE%B9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：杂散电容"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%84%E7%94%9F%E7%94%B5%E5%AE%B9" title="寄生电容">寄生电容</a></div>
<p>任意两个相邻导体，除非长久保持很近的距离，其电容通常很微小，但仍旧可以被视为电容器。这不受欢迎的效应称为“杂散电容”。原本各自孤立的电路，由于杂散电容的作用，可能会让两个电路互相干扰对方的信号，这效应称为<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%B2%E6%93%BE" class="mw-redirect" title="串扰">串扰</a>。杂散电容是电路在<a href="/wiki/%E7%9F%AD%E6%B3%A2" title="短波">短波波段</a>正常操作的限制因子。
</p><p>为了消除跟远方形成的杂散电容，可以将电路装置于金属机壳内，再将金属机壳跟<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%B0%E7%BA%BF" class="mw-redirect" title="地线">地线</a>连结。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E7.B0.A1.E5.96.AE.E7.B3.BB.E7.B5.B1.E7.9A.84.E9.9B.BB.E5.AE.B9"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="簡單系統的電容">简单系统的电容</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%BB%E5%AE%B9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="编辑章节：简单系统的电容"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>欲求得一个系统的电容，必须先解析<a href="/wiki/%E6%8B%89%E6%99%AE%E6%8B%89%E6%96%AF%E6%96%B9%E7%A8%8B%E5%BC%8F" class="mw-redirect" title="拉普拉斯方程">拉普拉斯方程</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \nabla ^{2}\phi =0}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <msup>
          <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x2207;<!-- ∇ --></mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mn>2</mn>
          </mrow>
        </msup>
        <mi>&#x03D5;<!-- ϕ --></mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \nabla ^{2}\phi =0}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/046b1f213d422442e4710eb5d4927f67d58953e2" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:8.636ex; height:3.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \nabla ^{2}\phi =0}"></span>，并且满足其边界条件，即在每一个导体表面的电势<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \phi }">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>&#x03D5;<!-- ϕ --></mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \phi }</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/72b1f30316670aee6270a28334bdf4f5072cdde4" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.385ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \phi }"></span>为某不同的已设定常数。对于具有高对称性的案例，这方法很简单。但是，对于较复杂案例，可能不存在以基本函数表示的解答。
</p><p>对于准二维问题，不同的几何构形之间可以用解析函数互相<a href="/wiki/%E6%98%A0%E5%B0%84" title="映射">映射</a>。详尽细节，请参阅条目<a href="/wiki/%E6%96%BD%E7%93%A6%E8%8C%A8-%E5%85%8B%E9%87%8C%E6%96%AF%E6%89%98%E8%B4%B9%E5%B0%94%E6%98%A0%E5%B0%84" title="施瓦茨-克里斯托费尔映射">施瓦茨-克里斯托费尔映射</a>
</p>

<h2><span id=".E8.8B.B1.E6.96.87.E5.90.8D.E7.A8.B1"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="英文名稱">英文名称</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%BB%E5%AE%B9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="编辑章节：英文名称"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>电容的英文也称为Capacity。但现在Capacity又另有<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%B5%E9%87%8F" class="mw-redirect" title="电量">电量</a>的意思。<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.8F.83.E9.96.B1"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="參閱">参阅</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%BB%E5%AE%B9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="编辑章节：参阅"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<li><span class="ilh-all" data-orig-title="水力學類比" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-foreign-title="hydraulic analogy"><span class="ilh-page"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B0%B4%E5%8A%9B%E5%AD%B8%E9%A1%9E%E6%AF%94&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="水力学类比（页面不存在）">水力学类比</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/hydraulic_analogy" class="extiw" title="en:hydraulic analogy"><span lang="en" dir="auto">hydraulic analogy</span></a></span>）</span></span></li>
